\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{raylib_2src_2external_2rgif_8h_source_l00012}00012\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ dithering.\ (It\ does\ at\ least\ use\ delta\ encoding\ -\/\ only\ the\ changed\ portions\ of\ each\ }}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{raylib_2src_2external_2rgif_8h_source_l00016}00016\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ as\ a\ quick\ and\ easily-\/integrated\ way\ for\ programs\ to\ spit\ out\ animations.}}
